========================================
  SuperTUI is ready!
========================================

KEYBOARD SHORTCUTS:
  Ctrl+1, Ctrl+2, Ctrl+3   Switch workspaces
  Ctrl+Left/Right          Previous/Next workspace
  Tab / Shift+Tab          Switch widget focus
  Ctrl+Q                   Quit

WIDGET CONTROLS:
  Counter: Up/Down arrows  Increment/Decrement
  Counter: R               Reset to zero
  Notes: Type freely       Text persists across workspace switches!

FEATURES TO TEST:
  â€¢ Focus indicator        Focused widget has cyan border
  â€¢ State preservation     Counter values persist when switching workspaces
  â€¢ Resizable panels       Drag the gray splitters (Workspace 1)
  â€¢ Multiple instances     Each counter widget has independent state
